<br /><br />
Broadcast Live from the Beverly Hilton Hotel on the HLN Network<br />
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"><tbody>
<tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-qA1wB2f2pVc/Ub8cpNdfO3I/AAAAAAAAe08/XeIeonYZMls/s1600/2KristenAlderson.JPG" style="clear: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-qA1wB2f2pVc/Ub8cpNdfO3I/AAAAAAAAe08/XeIeonYZMls/s320/2KristenAlderson.JPG" width="213" /></a></td></tr>
<tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">Kristen Alderson with the Outstanding Younger Actress In A Drama Series award for 'General Hospital' </td></tr>
</tbody></table>
Los Angeles, CA - June 16, 2013 - The National Academy of Television Arts and Sciences (NATAS) <span id="goog_563201108"></span><span id="goog_563201109"></span>tonight announced the winners of the 40th Annual Daytime Entertainment Emmy&#174; Awards in a sold-out gala for over 1,000 attendees at the Beverly Hilton Hotel in Beverly Hills, Los Angeles.<br />
<br />
"What an exciting night for the 40th Anniversary of the Daytime Entertainment Emmy&#174; Awards, said Malachy Wienges, Chairman, NATAS.&nbsp; "Daytime television is well and prospering as witnessed by this overwhelming turnout honoring the best that television can be.&nbsp; Working with our production and broadcast partners, LocoDistro and the HLN Network, we've delivered an evening that truly honors the outstanding work that happens day in and day out across all the genres that make up the Daytime viewer experience."<br />
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: right; margin-left: 1em; text-align: right;"><tbody>
<tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-pJA-b6aXceA/Ub8damz-hxI/AAAAAAAAe1M/av8TVKuqLH4/s1600/3CarrieFisherGeorgeLucas.JPG" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-pJA-b6aXceA/Ub8damz-hxI/AAAAAAAAe1M/av8TVKuqLH4/s320/3CarrieFisherGeorgeLucas.JPG" width="213" /></a></td></tr>
<tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><div class="MsoPlainText">
Carrie Fisher, George Lucas with the Outstanding Special
Class Animated Program award for 'Star Wars: The Clone Wars' </div>
</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GgQ4A-04frc/Ub8fF1CsvbI/AAAAAAAAe1Y/ANXsT6O7lxg/s1600/4MalachyWiengesGeorgeLucas.Jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"></a></div>
Sam Champion, anchor, <i>Good Morning America</i>, AJ Hammer, host, <i>HLN Showbiz Tonight</i>, and Robin Meade, host, "HLN Morning Express, hosted this evening's festivities including a pre-show, red carpet special featuring one-on-one interviews with the night's biggest stars.&nbsp; Among the night's many celebrity presenters were Alex Trebek of "Jeopardy!," Kathy Griffin, "My Life on the D-List," Wayne Brady, "Let's Make A Deal," Steve Harvey, "The Steve Harvey Show," Rachael Ray, "The Rachael Ray Show," Erika Slezak, <i>One Life to Live</i>, Corin Bernsen, <i>LA Law</i> and <i>The Young amd the Restless</i>, Bethenny Frankel, "The Bethenny Frankel Show," Dr. Drew Pinsky, "Dr. Drew," Kris Jenner, "Kris," Giada De Laurentis, "Giada at Home,"and Julie Chen, Sara Gilbert, Leah Remini, Aisha Tyler and Sheryl Underwood, "The Talk."<br />
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: right; margin-left: 1em; text-align: right;"><tbody>
<tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GgQ4A-04frc/Ub8fF1CsvbI/AAAAAAAAe1Y/ANXsT6O7lxg/s1600/4MalachyWiengesGeorgeLucas.Jpg" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GgQ4A-04frc/Ub8fF1CsvbI/AAAAAAAAe1Y/ANXsT6O7lxg/s320/4MalachyWiengesGeorgeLucas.Jpg" width="213" /></a></td></tr>
<tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><div class="MsoPlainText">
Malachy Wienges, George Lucas with the Outstanding
Special Class Animated Program award for 'Star Wars: The Clone Wars' </div>
</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<br />
<br />
One of the many highlights of the evening was the presentation of the Lifetime Achievement Award to two<span id="goog_563201144"></span><span id="goog_563201145"></span><br />
game show icons, Monty Hall of the original "Let's Make A Deal," and legendary producer, Bob Stewart, of "The Price is Right," "Password," and <i>Pyramid</i> fame.<br />
Wayne Brady, who is the present host of Monty Hall's famous "Let's Make A Deal, presented him with the honor.&nbsp;<br />
<table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"><tbody>
<tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-LXc5NZXGEG0/Ub8hOBrksxI/AAAAAAAAe18/zzkKDgVh8yI/s1600/6MontyHall.JPG" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-LXc5NZXGEG0/Ub8hOBrksxI/AAAAAAAAe18/zzkKDgVh8yI/s320/6MontyHall.JPG" width="213" /></a></td></tr>
<tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">Monty Hall with The Lifetime Achievement Award </span></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
The one and only Betty White, who worked with Bob Stewart and was a dear friend, presented the honor to Stewart's son, Sande, in a touching tribute.<br />
Stewart passed away last year at the age of ninety-one.<br />
<br />
In addition, the teenage sensation, "IL VOLO," performed their hit "Mas Que Amor," in the "In Memoriam" tribute and Carrie Fisher of <i>Star Wars</i> fame gave out the "Outstanding Special Class Animation" Emmy&#174; Award.<br />
<br />
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"><tbody>
<tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-nZL7MtCD1m0/Ub8gKmh5vFI/AAAAAAAAe1o/d9vyGjL13gs/s1600/5DrMehmetOz.JPG" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-nZL7MtCD1m0/Ub8gKmh5vFI/AAAAAAAAe1o/d9vyGjL13gs/s320/5DrMehmetOz.JPG" width="187" /></a></td></tr>
<tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">Mehmet Oz with the Outstanding Talk Show
Informative award for <i>The Dr. Oz Show</i> </span></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
The Daytime Entertainment Emmy&#174; Awards recognize outstanding achievement in all fields of daytime <br />
television production and are presented to individuals and programs broadcast from 2:00 a.m.-6:00 p.m. during the 2012 calendar year.<br />
The 40th Annual Daytime Entertainment Emmy&#174; Awards is a presentation of the National Academy of Television Arts &amp; Sciences in cooperation with the Academy of Television Arts and Sciences.<br />
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"><tbody>
<tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-zp5O1YLK_vQ/Ub8hyA71-nI/AAAAAAAAe2E/ROgtJWjy_2o/s1600/7WBMHallMW.jpg" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><img border="0" height="213" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-zp5O1YLK_vQ/Ub8hyA71-nI/AAAAAAAAe2E/ROgtJWjy_2o/s320/7WBMHallMW.jpg" width="320" /></a></td></tr>
<tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">Wayne Brady, Monty Hall, Malachy Wienges with
The Lifetime Achievement Award </span></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
A breakdown of the awards by network, as compiled by the independent accounting firm of Lutz and Carr, LLP, follows.<br />

About The National Academy of Television Arts and Sciences<br />
<br />
The National Academy of Television Arts &amp; Sciences (NATAS) is a professional service organization dedicated to the advancement of the arts and sciences of television and the promotion of creative leadership for artistic, educational and technical achievements within the television industry.<br />
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"><tbody>
<tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-K_bEha8UVzU/Ub8qbObDwoI/AAAAAAAAe20/ujoQJfdcysE/s1600/10ChandlerMassey.JPG" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-K_bEha8UVzU/Ub8qbObDwoI/AAAAAAAAe20/ujoQJfdcysE/s320/10ChandlerMassey.JPG" width="213" /></a></td></tr>
<tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">Chandler Massey with the Outstanding Younger
Actor In A Drama Series award for 'Days of Our Lives' </span></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<br />
Recognizing excellence in television with the coveted Emmy&#174; Award for News and Documentary, Sports, Daytime Entertainment, Daytime Creative Arts and Entertainment, Public &amp; Community Service, and Technology &amp; Engineering. Regional Emmy&#174; Awards are given in 19 regions across the United States. Emmy&#174; Awards given out for primetime programming are presented by our sister organization, the<span id="goog_563201172"></span><span id="goog_563201173"></span> Academy of Television Arts &amp; Science (ATAS). Beyond awards, NATAS has extensive educational programs including Regional Student Television and its Student Award for Excellence for outstanding journalistic work by high school students, as well as scholarships, publications, and major activities for both industry professionals and the viewing public.&nbsp; For more information, please visit the website at <a href="http://www.emmyonline.tv/">www.emmyonline.tv</a> <br />

<u><i><b>About HLN</b></i></u><br />
HLN is the national television network that focuses on the &#8220;must-see, must-share&#8221; stories of the day. Drawing upon the network's deep bench of talent, including Robin Meade, Jane Velez-Mitchell, Nancy Grace, Dr. Drew Pinsky and AJ Hammer, HLN dissects and demystifies the news stories and newsmakers people are talking about.<br />
<table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;"><tbody>
<tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-H6E8SYP7BfI/Ub8sagNvejI/AAAAAAAAe3U/rAGEWUmeR78/s1600/12DaysofOurLivesCast.jpg" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><img border="0" height="213" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-H6E8SYP7BfI/Ub8sagNvejI/AAAAAAAAe3U/rAGEWUmeR78/s320/12DaysofOurLivesCast.jpg" width="320" /></a></td></tr>
<tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-language: AR-SA; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-bidi; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-language: EN-US; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">'The Days of Our Lives' cast and producers with
the Outstanding Drama Series award for 'The Days Of Our Lives'</span></td></tr>

<br />
<a href="http://hlntv.com/">HLNtv.com</a>, the network's new digital platform, is the online destination for users to go deeper into the top stories driving the conversation and generating the national buzz.<br />
HLN is a CNN Worldwide network reaching more than 100 million households in the U.S. CNN Worldwide, a division of Turner Broadcasting System, Inc., a Time Warner Company, is the most trusted source for news and information.<br />

<u><i><b>LocoDistro</b></i></u><br />
LocoDistro (originally launched as Locomotive Distribution, Inc.) offers boutique attention to television and film clients, combining the strongest attributes of a production company, an international distribution company, a packaging agent, and a brand identity firm.<br />
For our acquisitions partners we offer a full slate of both narrative and documentary feature films as well as scripted and unscripted TV programming. Based in New York City, our team represents a blend of creative power, audience insight and financial discipline. Our team members are not only experts in what audiences respond to, but also experts in how to reach these audiences most effectively. <a href="http://www.locomotivegroup.com/">www.locomotivegroup.com</a><br />

 you to ALL ARTISTS mentioned in this blog for the gifts you have given to the world and continue

<span style="font-size: small;">With grateful XOXOXs ,</span><br />

<br />
<span style="font-size: x-small;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-eKUARMRxxs8/T3i_xsRrE1I/AAAAAAAAO18/O-4l7II65I8/s1600/1RichardS.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-eKUARMRxxs8/T3i_xsRrE1I/AAAAAAAAO18/O-4l7II65I8/s1600/1RichardS.jpg" /></a></span><br />
<div style="font-family: Georgia,&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;">
<div class="MsoNormal">
<br />
Please check out my blog celebrating Carol Channing
and why I feel she deserves the 2013 Kennedy Center Honor. </div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
<a href="http://richardskipper.blogspot.com/2013/05/carol-channing-deserves-2013-kennedy.html">http://richardskipper.blogspot.com/2013/05/carol-channing-deserves-2013-kennedy.html</a><br />
<br />
&nbsp;Thank
 you Terry LaBolt&#65279;: I would love to see Carol Channing receive the 
Kennedy Center honor, wouldn't you? Please consider signing. Carol's 50+
 years of bringing live theatre out on the road to practically every 
city in the US has been a rare gift to so many who might never have seen
 a live show otherwise. I was there for more than 1000 performances of 
HELLO, DOLLY. She never missed a performance. And she always delivered 
with an amazing energy that no one else I have ever worked with 
possessed; and I mean superhuman energy. Performing with her was like 
being shot out of a cannon - the only description I can think of that 
comes close. That energy was so powerful that it is still with me every 
single day. I think it was even one of the things that kept me alive 
through several rough patches. Please consider signing this; we're so 
close!<br />
<br />
<br />
<div class="MsoNormal">
<a href="http://www.change.org/petitions/the-kennedy-center-honors-give-carol-channing-a-2013-kennedy-center-honor">http://www.change.org/petitions/the-kennedy-center-honors-give-carol-channing-a-2013-kennedy-center-honor</a></div>

<div class="MsoNormal">
<span style="font-family: Broadway; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%;">Richard Skipper Celebrates Jackie Joseph: LIVE at The Metropolitan
Room in NYC </span></div>
<div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center;">
<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: red;">JULY 3<sup>rd</sup> at 7PM</span></b>!</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
<br /></div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
&nbsp;A benefit for <a href="http://www.actorsandothers.com/">Actors and Others For Animals</a> </div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-RYTBEhY2Ps0/Ub9JrksQ10I/AAAAAAAAe50/NU3BcEMZmiY/s1600/jackie-joseph-05.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-RYTBEhY2Ps0/Ub9JrksQ10I/AAAAAAAAe50/NU3BcEMZmiY/s1600/jackie-joseph-05.jpg" /></a></div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
Richard Skipper is Launching a new talk show in cabaret
based on his blog, <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">Richard Skipper
Celebrates</i>&#8230; Each show will be Celebrating artists and their &#8220;bodies of <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">worth</i>&#8221;. Richard&#8217;s first guest is
character actress Jackie Joseph. Each show will benefit the artist guest&#8217;s
charity of choice. The first will benefit Actors and Others for Animals.</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
Richard and Jackie will sit down for an intimate chat to
discuss her career and life and the people she has worked with for the first
forty-five minutes in a <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">VERY RARE</b>
New York appearance!</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
Imagine "Inside the Actor's Studio" but with
Richard Skipper's own personal style.</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
The last fifteen minutes will be comprised of questions from
the audience.</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1ONxkz_vLPk/Ub9J45YfDqI/AAAAAAAAe6A/scM-ABGSVx0/s1600/Jackie-Joseph-29c4c.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1ONxkz_vLPk/Ub9J45YfDqI/AAAAAAAAe6A/scM-ABGSVx0/s1600/Jackie-Joseph-29c4c.jpg" /></a></div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
Jackie will meet and greet the audience downstairs
afterward.</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
<span style="font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 14.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt;">Jackie Joseph</span><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> </span>is
an American character actress, voice artist, and writer known for <span id="goog_563201274"></span><span id="goog_563201275"></span>portraying
Alan Brady's niece Jackie on the <i>Dick van Dyke Show</i>, as well as the film
characters of: Audrey Fulquard in the original The Little Shop of Horrors,
Sheila Futterman in both Gremlins films, and the voice of Melody in the
animated television series <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Josie and the
Pussycats</b> and <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Josie and the
Pussycats in Outer Space</b>. </div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
Jackie was a regular on <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">The Doris Day Show</i></b> portraying Doris'
friend, Jackie Parker and also famously played the love interest of Ernest T.
Bass on The Andy Griffith Show as well as Imogene Harris, the eccentric
love-interest of Mario (Bob Denver) in Who's Minding The Mint&#8230;THAT&#8217;S JUST FOR
STARTERS!</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
*****</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
RICHARD SKIPPER<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>is a
Storyteller! He is also a popular entertainer, theater historian and pop
culture blogger. He has conducted over 500 interviews for his daily blog
celebrating people in the arts and is currently writing a book to coincide with
the <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">50th
Anniversary of Hello, Dolly!</i></b>, based also in part on his award-winning
callondolly.com website chronicling the Broadway classic. He has covered
several opening nights as the voice of Feinstein&#8217;s at Loews Regency and has
conducted on-stage interviews for <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Carol
Channing, Tommy Tune, Ron Young</b> and <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Peggy
Pope</b> at <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Barnes &amp; Noble</b> and
Queensboro Community College. (RichardSkipper.com and CallonDolly.com ) 2013
has been a breakout year for Richard. </div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3k-mq163S18/Ub9LvGUxyZI/AAAAAAAAe6c/cN-nzBe4glM/s1600/19ichrd.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="212" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3k-mq163S18/Ub9LvGUxyZI/AAAAAAAAe6c/cN-nzBe4glM/s320/19ichrd.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
Richard was the associate producer of the
2010, 2012, 2013 Bistro Awards. He recently produced Peggy Herman&#8217;s CD Release
Party at Feinsteins, directed by Peter Glebo and Tommy Tune, and it was an SRO
success. <br />
<div class="MsoNormal">
He produced <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Pamela
Luss&#8217;</b> run at The Metropolitan Room, NYC which was a huge success. Richard
can be seen in Dori Berenstein's CAROL CHANNING: LARGER THAN LIFE. Richard is
now focused mostly on his writing and producing this year. He has a highly
successful blog called RICHARD SKIPPER CELEBRATES, focusing on Artists and
their body of "Worth" and what makes a great UNIQUE entertainer! </div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
<br /></div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
(<a href="http://www.actorsandothers.com/">http://www.actorsandothers.com</a>).
</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
$20.00. Cover ($15.00 of every cover goes to Actors and
Others for Animals)/Two drink minimum. Reservations a MUST: 34 W 22nd
St&nbsp;&nbsp;New York, NY 10010</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
http://metropolitanroom.com/show.cfm?cart&amp;id=104228 </div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
<span style="font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 16.0pt; line-height: 115%;">(212) 206-0440</span></div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
Also&#8230;a<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>chance to win
a fabulous gift basket!</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
Please call with any questions you may have 845-365-0720</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
See Jackie Joseph in the ORIGINAL Little Shop of Horrors: <a href="http://youtu.be/IV4N3UdQxAI">http://youtu.be/IV4N3UdQxAI</a></div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
For a request to interview Jackie Joseph, please contact
Richard Skipper at 845-365-0720</div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
<br /></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-xhpaNViyuMg/Ub9Kp1QFDFI/AAAAAAAAe6Q/fNwJ32_6b10/s1600/Jackie-Joseph-1970s.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-xhpaNViyuMg/Ub9Kp1QFDFI/AAAAAAAAe6Q/fNwJ32_6b10/s1600/Jackie-Joseph-1970s.jpg" /></a></div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
<br /></div>
<div class="MsoNormal">
<br /></div>
<br />
<br />
<br />
<b><span style="color: black; font-size: small; line-height: 115%;"><i>NO COPYRIGHT INFRINGEMENT   INTENDED.&nbsp; FOR   ENTERTAINMENT   PURPOSES ONLY!</i></span></b></div>
<div style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">
<br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
<div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 101.25pt;">
&#8220;<i><b><span style="color: red;">When it comes to the history of
Jerry Herman&#8217;s brilliant production, beyond the 5000 plus performances of my own,
even I turn to Richard Skipper when I have questions about the remarkable
ladies who followed me in the role that the world fell in love with over 50
years ago</span>.</b></i>&#8221;-Carol Channing</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--GRBf8LNBBw/Ub9KVTykUHI/AAAAAAAAe6I/jfo-G-O-fac/s1600/%2524%2528KGrHqJ%252C%2521iYF%252132gV%2529tNBQU7J3zrFQ%257E%257E60_57.JPG.jpeg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--GRBf8LNBBw/Ub9KVTykUHI/AAAAAAAAe6I/jfo-G-O-fac/s320/%2524%2528KGrHqJ%252C%2521iYF%252132gV%2529tNBQU7J3zrFQ%257E%257E60_57.JPG.jpeg" width="242" /></a></div>
<i><b><span style="color: red;"></span></b></i><br />
<span style="font-size: small;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></div>
<div style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">

</div><div class='widget Profile' id='Profile1'>
<h2>About Me</h2>
<div class='widget-content'>
<a href='https://plus.google.com/112153842800169741032'><img alt='My Photo' class='profile-img' height='80' src='//lh5.googleusercontent.com/-PEb9AYFZsfc/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAePQ/TDdxmuZacp4/s512-c/photo.jpg' width='80'/></a>
<dl class='profile-datablock'>
<dt class='profile-data'>
<a class='profile-name-link g-profile' href='https://plus.google.com/112153842800169741032' rel='author' style='background-image: url(//www.google.com/images/icons/ui/gprofile_button-16.png);'>
Richard Skipper
</a>
<br/>
<div class='g-follow' data-annotation='bubble' data-height='20' data-href='https://plus.google.com/112153842800169741032'></div>
</dt>
<dd class='profile-textblock'>

<p>Richard Skipper has received artistic and critical acclaim
over the past 19 years as a first class entertainer. 2012 has been a breakout
year for Richard. When he closed his off-Broadway tribute to Carol Channing in
February 2011, it had garnered Richard 25 rave reviews! Richard was the
associate producer of the 2010, 2012, 2013 Bistro Awards. He recently produced
Peggy Herman&#8217;s CD Release Party at Feinsteins, directed by Peter Glebo and
Tommy Tune, and it was an SRO success. He also promoted <span>&#160;</span>jazz singer Pamela Luss&#8217; run at The
Metropolitan Room, NYC. Richard can be seen in Dori Berenstein&#39;s CAROL
CHANNING: LARGER THAN LIFE. In 2011, Richard debuted &quot;To Carol Channing
With Love&quot; at Blame It On Midnight in Palm Springs. Carol and her husband,
the late Harry Kullijian were in attendance. Richard is now focused mostly on
his writing and producing this year. He has a highly successful blog called <a href="http://richardskipper.blogspot.com/">RICHARD SKIPPER CELEBRATES</a>,
focusing on Artists and their body of &quot;Worth&quot; and what makes a great
UNIQUE entertainer! He is currently writing a book celebrating the 50th
anniversary of <i>Hello, Dolly!</i> </p>

<p>Richard continues to teach his workshops on CREATING HIGHER VISIBILITY
utilizing social media. He has served on several panels on the business end of
show business and is often asked to emcee many prestigious events. He is
campaigning diligently for Carol Channing to receive a long over due Kennedy
Center Honor in 2013. He also continues to raise money for The Dr. Carol
Channing-Harry Kullijian Foundation For The Arts, Established in 2005 with the
hopes of bringing the importance of arts education to the general public,
provide music instruments for underfunded public schools and scholarships for
California State University students. Richard&#39;s appearances continue to be
sell-outs. Richard is also available for one-on-one consultations which afford
you the personal time with him catering specifically and only to your needs. </p>

<p>Other highlights include performing the role of Dolly Levi as Carol Channing
at Asbury Park&#39;s Paramount Theater in a special benefit performance of
&quot;Hello Dolly!&quot; with a cast of 125 and a 25 piece orchestra; a Theatre
Wing tribute to Carol Channing, Tommy Tune and James Earl Jones; benefit
performances for the Dr. Carol Channing Harry Kullijian Foundation For The Arts
with Carol and Harry in attendance and special guest star Neil Sedaka! Richard
also serves on the board of the Foundation as the east coast representative.
Richard has appeared on board WindStar Cruise Lines from Rome to Athens, and
several return engagements in celebration of Carol Channing&#39;s birthdays at
Washington DC&#39;s National Theater. He has appeared at Carnegie Hall with Sam
Harris and The New York City Gay Men&#39;s Chorus, Late Night With Conan O&#39;Brien,
and an appearance with Carol Channing and the San Francisco Gay Men&#39;s Chorus at
the Palace Of Fine Arts in San Francisco. </p>

<p>Richard Skipper has taken his tribute to Carol Channing to Atlantic City for
three long-running engagements at Trump&#39;s Taj Mahal and The Hilton. He has
played three engagements at Caesar&#39;s Casino Windsor in Windsor, Ontario and The
Windsor Hilton. Other engagements include The Ice Palace on Fire Island (for
which he won two Mikey Awards for best act on Fire Island), St. Luke&#39;s Theatre,
The Bradstan Inn (in the Catskills), Georgian Court College (with Dody
Goodman), The Ocean&#39;s Inn and The New Crown And Anchor in Provincetown, MA;
Tavern On The Green and The Russian Tea Room. He was the featured performer for
Pridefest in Milwaukee along with Pat Benatar and Judy Tenuta. </p>

<p>Richard Skipper has also performed at the 21 Club at the request of Arlene
Dahl, The Regent (special performance for Carol Channing!), Le Cirque for Joey
Adams&#39; 85th Birthday; on numerous occasions for the NY Post&#39;s gossip columnist
Cindy Adams; as a guest star in &quot;The Impersonators&quot; with Jamie deRoy
at The Friar&#39;s Club, The New York Historical Society with Claire Bloom, Donna
McKechnie, Hayley Mills, Tony Roberts, and George Shearing ; the &quot;Get Out
And Vote&quot; Rally for New Jersey&#39;s Senator Lautenberg with Dr. Quinn&#39;s Chad
Allen, Activist James Dale &amp; Rue McClanahan; and he has also shared the
stage with Carol Channing on more than one occasion. He has hosted Dancers Over
40&#8217;s Legacy Awards three times. </p>

<span>Richard Skipper donates portions of his appearances to
the Dr. Carol Channing/Harry Kullijian Foundation For The Arts. </span></dd>
</dl>
